.22b1		10 0b		bpl $22be			bpl done_handle_events				; Nothing to do

.22b6		b0 06		bcs $22be			bcs done_handle_events				; If Carry is set, skip the handler
.22b8		20 bf 22	jsr $22bf			jsr dispatch						; Handle the event

.22bf						dispatch:

.22c1		c9 52		cmp #$52			cmp #kernel.event.timer.EXPIRED		; is the event timer.EXPIRED?
.22c3		f0 32		beq $22f7			beq UpdateScreen					; run the screen update

.22c7		f0 01		beq $22ca			beq setJoyStick

.22ca		a5 a4		lda $a4				lda event.joystick.joy1

.22d1		9c fe 2a	stz $2afe			stz joyY
.22d4		9c ff 2a	stz $2aff			stz joyB
.22d7						jUp:

.22d9		29 01		and #$01			and #$01							; check for up
.22db		f0 05		beq $22e2			beq jDown							; if not up skip to test down
.22dd		ce fe 2a	dec $2afe			dec joyY							; if up dec joy Y direction to $ff
.22e0		80 09		bra $22eb			bra jButton							; skip down test
.22e2						jDown:
.22e2		a5 d8		lda $d8				lda $d8								; reload joystick state
.22e4		29 02		and #$02			and #$02							; check for down
.22e6		f0 03		beq $22eb			beq jButton							; if not down skip
.22e8		ee fe 2a	inc $2afe			inc joyY							; incrment Joy y direction to $01
.22eb						jButton:
.22eb		a5 d8		lda $d8				lda $d8								; reload joystick state
.22ed		29 10		and #$10			and #$10							; check for button 0
.22ef		f0 05		beq $22f6			beq jDone							; no button, we are done
.22f1		a9 01		lda #$01			lda #$01
.22f3		8d ff 2a	sta $2aff			sta joyB							; yes botton, set joy B to 1
